         +: ReplyLocale {

      1004 +function normalizeServiceName(s: string): string[] {         
      1005 +  const stripDiacritics = s                                  
      1006 +    .normalize('NFD')                                        
      1007 +    .replace(/[ŐÄ-ÕĮ]/g, '')                                     
      1008 +    .replace(/Ňā/gi, 'l')                                     
      1009 +    .replace(/—Ď/gi, '–Ķ')                                     
      1010 +  const STOP = new Set([                                     
      1011 +    '–ł',                                                     
      1012 +    '–Ĺ–į',                                                    
      1013 +    '—Ā',                                                     
      1014 +    '–ī–Ľ—Ź',                                                   
      1015 +    '–ĺ—ā',                                                    
      1016 +    '–ī–ĺ',                                                    
      1017 +    '–Ī–Ķ–∑',                                                   
      1018 +    'usŇāuga',                                                
      1019 +    'serwis',                                                
      1020 +    'service',                                               
      1021 +    '—É—Ā–Ľ—É–≥–į',                                                
      1022 +    'salonu',                                                
      1023 +    'cena',                                                  
      1024 +    'price',                                                 
      1025 +    'oraz',                                                  
      1026 +    'pl',                                                    
      1027 +    'ru',                                                    
      1028 +    'en',                                                    
      1029 +  ])                                                         
      1030 +  return stripDiacritics                                     
      1031 +    .toLowerCase()                                           
      1032 +    .replace(/[^a-z–į-—Ź—Ď—Ė—ó\s+]/giu, ' ')                      
      1033 +    .split(/\s+/)                                            
      1034 +    .filter((w) => w.length >= 3 && !STOP.has(w))            
      1035 +}                                                            
      1036 +                                                             
      1037 +/** Jaccard-similarity –Ņ–ĺ —ā–ĺ–ļ–Ķ–Ĺ–į–ľ [0..1]. */                 
      1038 +function tokenSimilarity(a: string[], b: string[]): number { 
      1039 +  if (a.length === 0 || b.length === 0) return 0             
      1040 +  const sa = new Set(a)                                      
      1041 +  const sb = new Set(b)                                      
      1042 +  let inter = 0                                              
      1043 +  for (const x of sa) if (sb.has(x)) inter++                 
      1044 +  const union = sa.size + sb.size - inter                    
      1045 +  return inter / union                                       
      1046 +}

      1122 +  const rows = useMemo<PriceMatchRow[]>(() => {

           +ull

           +ull

           + s + x, 0) / prices.length : null

           + ?? 0))

      584 +  function toggle(id: string) {                               
      585 +    setPicked((prev) => {

      587 +      if (next.has(id)) next.delete(id)                       
      588 +      else next.add(id)                                       
      589 +      return next                                             
      590 +    })                                                        
      591 +  }

      594 +  }                                                           
      595 +  function clearAll() {

      1165 +// OccupancyTable ‚ÄĒ —Ā–Ľ–ĺ—ā—č –ļ–ĺ–Ĺ–ļ—É—Ä–Ķ–Ĺ—ā–ĺ–≤ –Ĺ–į –Ī–Ľ–ł–∂–į–Ļ—ą–ł–Ķ 7 –ī–Ĺ–Ķ–Ļ –Ņ–ĺ 
           +top-5 —É—Ā–Ľ—É–≥–į–ľ.

      1175 +                                                             
      1176 +function OccupancyTable({                                    
      1177 +  salonId,                                                   
      1178 +  competitors,                                               
      1179 +  snapshots,

      1181 +}: {

      1188 +  const [insights, setInsights] = useState<{ title: string; b
           +ody: string }[] | null>(null)                                
      1189 +                                                             
      1190 +  // –°–ĺ–Ī–ł—Ä–į–Ķ–ľ –Ņ–ĺ—Ā–Ľ–Ķ–ī–Ĺ–ł–Ļ occupancy-snapshot –Ĺ–į –ļ–į–∂–ī–ĺ–≥–ĺ –ļ–ĺ–Ĺ–ļ—É—Ä–Ķ
           +–Ĺ—ā–į.                                                         
      1191 +  const latestByCompetitor = useMemo(() => {                 
      1192 +    const map = new Map<string, NonNullable<typeof snapshots>
           +[number]>()

      1194 +      if (s.kind !== 'occupancy') continue                   
      1195 +      const prev = map.get(s.competitor_id)

      1198 +      }                                                      
      1199 +    }                                                        
      1200 +    return map                                               
      1201 +  }, [snapshots])                                            
      1202 +                                                             
      1203 +  // –£–Ņ–Ľ–ĺ—Č–į–Ķ–ľ: –ļ–į–∂–ī–į—Ź —Ā—ā—Ä–ĺ–ļ–į = (competitor √ó –Ķ–≥–ĺ —É—Ā–Ľ—É–≥–į-snaps
           +hot).                                                        
      1204 +  type Row = {

      1206 +    competitorName: string                                   
      1207 +    service: OccupancyService                                
      1208 +    totalStaff: number                                       
      1209 +  }                                                          
      1210 +  const rows = useMemo<Row[]>(() => {                        
      1211 +    const out: Row[] = []                                    
      1212 +    for (const c of competitors) {                           
      1213 +      const snap = latestByCompetitor.get(c.id)              
      1214 +      if (!snap) continue                                    
      1215 +      const data = snap.data as { services?: OccupancyService
           +[]; total_staff?: number }                                   
      1216 +      const services = Array.isArray(data.services) ? data.se
           +rvices : []                                                  
      1217 +      for (const svc of services) {                          
      1218 +        out.push({                                           
      1219 +          competitorId: c.id,                                
      1220 +          competitorName: c.name,                            
      1221 +          service: svc,                                      
      1222 +          totalStaff: data.total_staff ?? 0,                 
      1223 +        })                                                   
      1224 +      }                                                      
      1225 +    }

      1227 +  }, [competitors, latestByCompetitor])                      
      1228 +                                                             
      1229 +  // –°—Ä–Ķ–ī–Ĺ–Ķ–Ķ –Ņ–ĺ –≤—Ā–Ķ–ľ ‚ÄĒ –ī–Ľ—Ź % vs —Ā—Ä–Ķ–ī–Ĺ–ł–Ļ.                     
      1230 +  const avgSlotsByService = useMemo(() => {                  
      1231 +    const map = new Map<string, number>()                    
      1232 +    const buckets = new Map<string, number[]>()              
      1233 +    for (const r of rows) {                                  
      1234 +      const list = buckets.get(r.service.name) ?? []         
      1235 +      list.push(r.service.free_slots_7d)                     
      1236 +      buckets.set(r.service.name, list)                      
      1237 +    }                                                        
      1238 +    for (const [name, list] of buckets.entries()) {          
      1239 +      const avg = list.reduce((s, x) => s + x, 0) / list.leng
           +th                                                           
      1240 +      map.set(name, avg)                                     
      1241 +    }                                                        
      1242 +    return map                                               
      1243 +  }, [rows])                                                 
      1244 +

           +ssage : String(e)),                                          
      1262 +      },                                                     
      1263 +    )                                                        
      1264 +  }                                                          
      1265 +                                                             
      1266 +  return (                                                   
      1267 +    <div className="flex flex-col gap-3">                    
      1268 +      <div className="border-border bg-card shadow-finsm over
           +flow-x-auto rounded-lg border">

           + border-b text-[11px] uppercase tracking-wider">             
      1271 +            <tr>                                             
      1272 +              <th className="px-4 py-3 text-left font-semibol

      1273 +                {t('reports_hub.competitors.col_competitor')}
      1274 +              </th>

      1279 +                {t('reports_hub.competitors.col_staff_count')
           +}                                                            
      1280 +              </th>                                          
      1281 +              <th className="px-3 py-3 text-right font-semibo
           +ld">                                                         
      1282 +                {t('reports_hub.competitors.col_slots_7d')}  
      1283 +              </th>                                          
      1284 +              <th className="px-3 py-3 text-right font-semibo
           +ld">                                                         
      1285 +                {t('reports_hub.competitors.col_days_covered'
           +)}                                                           
      1286 +              </th>                                          
      1287 +              <th className="px-3 py-3 text-right font-semibo
           +ld">                                                         
      1288 +                {t('reports_hub.competitors.col_vs_avg')}    
      1289 +              </th>                                          
      1290 +            </tr>                                            
      1291 +          </thead>

           +')}                                                          
      1300 +                </td>                                        
      1301 +              </tr>

      1303 +              rows.map((r, i) => {                           
      1304 +                const avg = avgSlotsByService.get(r.service.n
           +ame) ?? 0

      1337 +                      )}
